           <h6 class="zsg-subfooter-header">
            Why use Zillow?
           </h6>
           <p>
            Zillow is perfect for searching homes for sale in the United States. By analyzing real estate information on millions of homes for sale across the United States, we calculate home values (Zestimates) and the Zillow Home Value Price Index.

                        <span data-target-id="zest-tip-table" class="zsg-tooltip-launch zsg-icon-circle-question">
                        </span>
                        <div class="zsg-tooltip" id="zest-tip-table">
                         A
                         <strong>
                          Zestimate
                         </strong>
                         home valuation is Zillow's estimated market value. It is not an appraisal. Use it as a starting point to determine a home's value.
                         <a href="/wikipages/What-is-a-Zestimate/" href="#">
                          Learn more
                         </a>
                         <br />
                         <br />
                         The
                         <strong>
                          Value Range
                         </strong>
                         is the high and low estimate market value for which Zillow values a home. The more information, the smaller the range, and the more accurate the Zestimate.
                         <a href="/howto/DataCoverageZestimateAccuracy.htm" href="#">
                          See data coverage and accuracy table
                         </a>
                         <br />
                         <br />
                         <strong>
                          Don't agree with your home's Zestimate?
                         </strong>
                         Owners can  edit their home facts  to make the Zestimate more accurate. Plus, you can leave an opinion on your Zestimate value below. Just click "Owner Estimate".
                        </div>

                  </a>
                 </p>
                 <div id="home-value-tooltip" class="zsg-tooltip home-value-tooltip">
                  <p>
                   The return values below are estimates based on the region, home facts, and past sales data.
        Your situation may vary based on current finish level of the room, changing style trends, depreciation,
        and how much of the project budget is invested in structural changes vs. functional/cosmetic improvements.

            </p>

             Homes with a Make Me Move
             <sup>
              &reg;
             </sup>
             price indicate the amount the owner(s) would be willing to sell for. They are exclusive to Zillow and a great way to learn about homes before they hit the market.
            </p>
